# Diatonic Modes

**Diatonic Modes: Chord Scales**

Lydian

- Computer:

  - \[0, 2, 4, 6, 7, 9, 11\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, 2, 3, \#4, 5, 6, 7

- Triads:

  - 1 maj, 2 maj, 3 min, \#4 dim, 5 maj, 6 min, 7 min

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 maj7, 2 dom7, 3 min7, \#4 min7(έβφ5), 5 maj7, 6 min7, 7 min7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 maj9, 2 dom9, 3 min9, \#4 min7(έβφ5έβφ9), 5 maj9, 6 min9, 7 min7(έβφ9)

Ionian (Major)

- Computer:

  - \[0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 11\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7

- Triads:

  - 1 maj, 2 min, 3 min, 4 maj, 5 maj, 6 min, 7 dim

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 maj7, 2 min7, 3 min7, 4 maj7, 5 dom7, 6 min7, 7 min7(έβφ5)

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 maj9, 2 min9, 3 min7(έβφ9), 4 maj9, 5 dom9, 6 min9, 7 min7(έβφ5έβφ9)

Mixolydian

- Computer:

  - \[0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 10\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, έβφ7

- Triads:

  - 1 maj, 2 min, 3 dim, 4 maj, 5 min, 6 min, έβφ7 maj

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 dom7, 2 min7, 3 min7(έβφ5), 4 maj7, 5 min7, 6 min7, έβφ7 maj7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 dom9, 2 min9, 3min7(έβφ5έβφ9), 4 maj9, 5 min9, 6 min7(έβφ9), έβφ7 maj9

Dorian

- Computer:

  - \[0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 9, 10\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, 2, έβφ 3, 4, 5, 6, έβφ7

- Triads:

  - 1 min, 2 min, έβφ3 maj, 4 maj, 5 min, 6 dim, έβφ7 maj

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 min7, 2 min7, έβφ3 maj7, 4 dom7 5 min7, 6 min7(έβφ5), έβφ7 maj7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 min9, 2 min7(έβφ9), έβφ3 maj9, 4 dom9, 5 min9, 6 min7(έβφ5έβφ9), έβφ7 maj9

Aeolian (Minor)

- Computer:

  - \[0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 8, 10\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, 2, έβφ3, 4, 5, έβφ6, έβφ7

- Triads:

  - 1 min, 2 min, έβφ3 maj, 4 min, 5 min, έβφ6 maj , έβφ7 maj

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 min7, 2 min7(έβφ5), έβφ3 maj7, 4 min7, 5 min7, έβφ6 maj7, έβφ7 dom7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 min9, 2 min7(έβφ5έβφ9), έβφ3 maj9, 4 min9, 5 min7(έβφ9), έβφ6 maj9, έβφ7 dom9

Phrygian

- Computer:

  - \[0, 1, 3, 5, 7, 8, 10\]

- Intervals:

  - 1, έβφ2, έβφ3, 4, 5, έβφ6, έβφ7

- Triads:

  - 1 min, έβφ2 maj, έβφ3 maj, 4 min, 5 dim, έβφ6 maj, έβφ7 min

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 min7, έβφ2 maj7, έβφ3 dom7, 4 min7, 5 min7(έβφ5), έβφ6 maj7, έβφ7 min7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 min7(έβφ9), έβφ2 maj9, έβφ3 dom9, 4 min9, 5 min7(έβφ5έβφ9), έβφ6 maj9, έβφ7 min9

Locrian

- Computer:

  - \[0, 1, 3, 5, 6, 8, 10\]

- Locrian Intervals:

  - 1, έβφ2, έβφ3, 4, έβφ5, έβφ6, έβφ7

- Triads:

  - 1 dim, έβφ2 maj , έβφ3 min, 4 min, έβφ5 maj,έβφ6 maj, έβφ7 min

- 7th Chords:

  - 1 min7(έβφ5), έβφ2 maj7, έβφ3 min7, 4 min7, έβφ5 maj7, έβφ6 dom7, έβφ7 min7

- 9th Chords:
  - 1 min7(έβφ5έβφ9), έβφ2 maj9, έβφ3 min9, 4 min7(έβφ9), έβφ5 maj9, έβφ6 dom9,έβφ7 min9

# Aeolian (Minor)

**C Aeolian (Minor)**

\#\#\# The key of "C Minor" has three flats.  
\#\#\#\# The notes of the scale are: C, D, Eέβφ, F, G, Aέβφ, Bέβφ

**F Aeolian (Minor)**

\#\#\# The key of "F Minor" has four flats.  
\#\#\#\# The notes of the scale are: F, G, Aέβφ, Bέβφ, C, Dέβφ, Eέβφ  
\#\#\#\# F Minor Scale \= F Aeolian Mode  
\#\#\#\#\# Parent Mode: Aέβφ Ionian  
\_component:sequence(4a8f85a9-9836-4505-b242-3fc856221e3d, piano)\_

The notes in a scale are used to create melodies, bass lines, and chords. Each scale has a distinct shape, or contour, across the keyboard.

Many melodies are created from a variation on the minor scale called the pentatonic scale.

\#\#\#\# The F Minor Pentatonic Scale has 5 notes: F, Aέβφ, Bέβφ, C, Eέβφ  
\_component:sequence(a0ff972f-1391-4bd3-83b1-729b65e8c407, piano)\_

# Relative Modes

**Relative Modes:**

- **Red**
  - C Ionian, D Dorian, E Phrygian, F Lydian, G Mixolydian, A Aeolian, B Locrian
- **Vermillion**
  - G Ionian, A Dorian, B Phrygian, C Lydian, D Mixolydian, E Aeolian, F\# Locrian
- **Orange**
  - D Ionian, E Dorian, F\# Phrygian, G Lydian, A Mixolydian, B Aeolian, C\# Locrian
- **Amber**
  - A Ionian, B Dorian, C\# Phrygian, D Lydian, E Mixolydian, F\# Aeolian, G\# Locrian
- **Green**
  - E Ionian, F\# Dorian, G\# Phrygian, A Lydian, B Mixolydian, C\# Aeolian, D\# Locrian
- **Sage**
  - B Ionian, C\# Dorian, D\# Phrygian, E Lydian, F\# Mixolydian, G\# Aeolian, A\# Locrian
- **Teal**
  - F\# Ionian, G\# Dorian, A\# Phrygian, B Lydian, C\# Mixolydian, E\# Aeolian, E\# Locrian
- **Blue**
  - Db Ionian, Eb Dorian, F Phrygian, Gb Lydian, Ab Mixolydian, Bb Aeolian, C Locrian
- **Indigo**
  - Ab Ionian, Bb Dorian, C Phrygian, Db Lydian, Eb Mixolydian, F Aeolian, G Locrian
- **Purple**
  - Eb Ionian, F Dorian, G Phrygian, Ab Lydian, Bb Mixolydian, C Aeolian, D Locrian
- **Magenta**
  - Bb Ionian, C Dorian, D Phrygian, Eb Lydian, F Mixolydian, G Aeolian, A Locrian
- **Pink**
  - F Ionian, G Dorian, A Phrygian, Bb Lydian, C Mixolydian, D Aeolian, E Locrian

**Collection: Parallel Modes**

C

- C Lydian, C Ionian, C Mixolydian, C Dorian, C Aeolian, C Phrygian, C Locrian, C Harmonic Major, C Ionian \#5, C Mixolydian έβφ6,
